display: inline-block; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1; font-family: FontAwesome; font-size: inherit; text-rendering: auto; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased;"></i><span> </span>@Guest</a><span data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span></div><span class="bookmarked" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; position: absolute; top: -2px; right: 6px; font-size: 16px; color: rgb(35, 144, 176); opacity: 0; transition: opacity 0.75s ease-in-out 0s;"><i class="fa fa-bookmark-o" style="box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 1; font-family: FontAwesome; font-size: inherit; text-rendering: auto; -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased;"></i></span></small></div><br data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div class="content" component="post/content" itemprop="text" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word; padding-bottom: 1px; margin-top: -43px; margin-left: 61px; overflow: hidden;"><p data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px;">@yeahhmonkey There are<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">a lot of files for weapons Data</strong>, so, you can use "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">Ctrl + F3</strong>" and check which of them have Knife DATA, then, take this data and put it on your DLC folder file respectivelly, an example:</p><ul data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><li data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; list-style-type: disc;">If there are 8 "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">shop_weapon.meta</strong>" using<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">Ctrl + F3</strong>,<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">check each one until you find the weapon data you're searching</strong>.<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">If no data</strong>, then don't put anything on the respective file of your "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">/common/data/file.meta</strong>". Do the same with all files, except "dlctext.meta", with this one don't do anything.</li></ul><p data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px;">I don't know if you understand what I'm trying to explain, but is not hard. Also, you can take a look at<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;"><a href="https://es.gta5-mods.com/weapons/mg-42-add-on-replace" rel="nofollow" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-color: transparent; color: rgb(32, 186, 78); text-decoration: none;">this mod</a></strong>,<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">is an Add-On weapon</strong><span> </span>(you can see how is structured each file).</p></div><div class="clearfix post-footer" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div component="post/signature" data-uid="97" class="post-signature" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 12px; border-top: 1px dashed rgb(222, 222, 222); padding: 5px 1px 1px; display: inline-block; font-style: italic; margin-left: 61px; max-width: 100%;"><p data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px;"><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">Join us in the<span> </span><a href="https://discord.gg/hwYVCmw" rel="nofollow" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-color: transparent; color: rgb(32, 186, 78); text-decoration: none;">5Mods Discord</a></strong><span> </span>-&gt; No GTA:Online. I want to replace my vehicles. I'm using the add-on to replace method. Step 7 is where I usually get confused. So, from my ford GT dlc.rpf I have extracted the nessesary meta files.<br data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;">I understand that I'm supposed to copy + paste the text from them into the meta files located in the "DLCFolderThatIChose".rpf.<br data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Now what I want to know is, do I copy the text inside &lt;item&gt;&lt;/item&gt; tags from the fordGT meta files and paste them within the parent tags of the destination meta file?<br data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Or can I simply copy everything inside it the FordGT meta file (including the "vehicleModelInfoVariation" &amp; "?XML version" etc tags) and paste it at the bottom of the destination meta files?<br data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Because the Ford GT has successfully replaced the bullet, and works well, but the tunning &amp; dials don't work.</li></ul><ul data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><li data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; list-style-type: disc;">Second question, inside the meta files for the Ford GT, I've noticed that it has fgt, fgt_modkit &amp; or &lt;modelName&gt;fgt&lt;/modelName&gt; keywords. Shouldn't I change them to bullet or something like that?<br data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;">I know that I'm supposed to to that for the handling meta, but I'm not too sure about the other metas.</li></ul><p data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px;">Thanks for clearing my doubts. overflow-wrap: break-word; padding-bottom: 1px; margin-top: -43px; margin-left: 61px; overflow: hidden;"><p data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px;"><a class="plugin-mentions-a" href="https://forums.gta5-mods.com/uid/1650" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-color: transparent; color: rgb(49, 112, 143); text-decoration: none; font-size: 0.9em; white-space: nowrap;">@Fearnoid</a></p><p data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px;"><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;"><em data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Answer to first question:</em></strong><span> </span>To get dials, lights and tuning working, search for the car name (if is Ford GT to Bullet, in each meta file (if are "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">fgt.ytd/.ytf</strong>" files, then search for "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">fgt</strong>") search it and copy from<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;Item&gt;</strong><span> </span>to<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;/Item&gt;</strong>. Also don't forget that in "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">carcols.meta</strong>" files sometimes there are<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">2 sections</strong>,<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;Kits&gt;&lt;/Kits&gt;</strong><span> </span>and<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;Lights&gt;&lt;/Lights&gt;</strong>. If so, copy both "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;Item&gt;</strong><span> </span>to<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;/Item&gt;</strong>" lines on their respective section.<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">ALSO</strong>, don't forget to replace the "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">fgt</strong>" word with "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">bullet</strong>" of the car you want to replace if you copy the entire<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;Item&gt;</strong><span> </span>to<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;/Item&gt;</strong><span> </span>lines).</p><p data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px;"><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;"><em data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Answer to second question:</em></strong><span> </span>For "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">handling.meta</strong>" file, first search by car name, and then, search and copy since the first line starting with "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;fMass</strong>" tag to the "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;/Item&gt;</strong>" tag. For "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">vehicles.meta</strong>", process is the same as for "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">handling.meta</strong>",<span> </span><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">BUT</strong>, searching and copying since the "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;expressionDictName&gt;</strong>" to the "<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">&lt;/Item&gt;</strong>" tag, and also don't forget to copy something like the next, but for the car you're replacing (<strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">this is in the final of the "vehicles.meta" file and is necessary to get working dials</strong>):</p><pre class="markdown-highlight" style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word; overflow: auto; font-size: 13px; line-height: 1.42857; display: block; color: inherit; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; padding: 9.5px; margin: 1rem 0px 10px; word-break: break-all; background-color: inherit; border: none; border-radius: 0px; max-height: 350px;"><code class="hljs xml" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: inherit; padding: 0.5em; border-radius: 0px; min-width: 100%;"> <span class="hljs-tag" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: navy; font-weight: 400;">&lt;<span class="hljs-name" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: navy; font-weight: 400;">Item</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: navy; font-weight: 400;">&lt;<span class="hljs-name" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: navy; font-weight: 400;">parent</span>&gt;</span>vehicles_futo_interior<span class="hljs-tag" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: navy; font-weight: 400;">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: navy; font-weight: 400;">parent</span>&gt;</span>

</code></pre><p data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px;">I don't know if I'm explained good (English isn't my native language), but please let me know if you understood what I told you or not.</p></div><div class="clearfix post-footer" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><div component="post/signature" data-uid="97" class="post-signature" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 12px; border-top: 1px dashed rgb(222, 222, 222); padding: 5px 1px 1px; display: inline-block; font-style: italic; margin-left: 61px; max-width: 100%;"><p data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px 0px 10px;"><strong data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-weight: 700;">Join us in the<span> </span><a href="https://discord.gg/hwYVCmw" rel="nofollow" data-immersive-translate-walked="80a75fda-8f3d-42b7-8fa3-3fadb71c7301" style="box-sizing: border-box; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; background-color: transparent; color: rgb(32, 186, 78); text-decoration: none;">5Mods Discord</a></strong><span> </span>-&gt; No GTA:Online. [Tutorial] How to do: Add-On / Replace (Vehicles & Weapons)
[教程]怎么做：添加/替换（车辆和武器）
[Reyser](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/user/reyser) [ MODERATOR](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/groups/global-moderators) [7 years ago](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/post/1234) 
Hello guys! This tutorial will help you to make the tedious GTA Modding a bit easier
大家好！本教程将帮助您使繁琐的 GTA 模组变得更容易一些
:)

If you want a simplified (With Screenshots) tutorial for vehicles: :arrow_right:[ Click me! ](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/post/29728):arrow_left:
如果您想要简化的 （ With Screenshots ） 车辆教程：点击我！

提高游戏性能的一些技巧：点击我！

西班牙语翻译 / Traducción Española： Click me！/点击！
WARNING: By reading this tutorial, you're accepting to reject any accusation against this tutorial or his owner for any damage you can cause to your game (Do it at your own risk). If you didn't read this before, do not relieve yourself from guilt.
WARNING ：阅读本教程，即表示您接受拒绝对本教程或其所有者的任何指控，因为您可能对您的游戏造成任何损害（风险自负）。如果你以前没有读过这篇文章，请不要让自己摆脱内疚。

That doesn't mean that you can't ask for help.
这并不意味着你不能寻求帮助。

Knowledge: What I need to know before asking for help?
Knowledge ： 在寻求帮助之前，我需要知道什么？
How can I fix this error?
如何修复此错误？

ERR_FIL_PACK_1: The total of vehicles that the game try to load is higher than the default limit, or you're using a SCRIPT mod that's incompatible with the most recent game version.
ERR_FIL_PACK_1 ：游戏尝试加载的车辆总数高于默认限制，或者您使用的 SCRIPT 模组与最新游戏版本不兼容。

How to fix that? Try to use one of the "gameconfig.xml" available on main GTA5-Mods website, or check that all your SCRIPT mods are compatible with the most recent game version.
如何解决这个问题？尝试使用GTA5-Mods主网站上提供的“gameconfig.xml”之一，或检查所有SCRIPT模组是否与最新的游戏版本兼容。
ERR_FIL_PACK_3: The size of 1 or more DLC's is higher or close to 4GB.
ERR_FIL_PACK_3 ：1 个或多个 DLC 的大小高于或接近 4GB。

How to fix that? Defragment "vehicles.rpf" and "dlc.rpf" files from the DLC/'s that's causing that error respectively. If this does not work it means that one or more of your dlc.rpf files have already reached a size limit and you'll need to move some mods to a brand new DLC folder.
如何解决这个问题？分别从导致该错误的 DLC/ 中对“vehicles.rpf”和“dlc.rpf”文件进行碎片整理。如果这不起作用，则意味着您的一个或多个 dlc.rpf 文件已达到大小限制，您需要将一些模组移动到全新的 DLC 文件夹中。
How can I spawn ADD-ON Vehicles or Weapons?
如何生成附加载具或武器？

If vehicle files are called "chevrolet.ytd/.ytf", in-game, use a trainer like [Enhanced Native Trainer](https://es.gta5-mods.com/scripts/enhanced-native-trainer) to spawn them. In this case, spawn will be "chevrolet".
如果车辆文件名为“chevrolet.ytd/.ytf”，则在游戏中，请使用 Enhanced Native Trainer 等训练器来生成它们。在这种情况下，生成将是“雪佛兰”。
For weapons, you will need to buy them in a Ammunation Store, can't be spawned (or I don't know how) through a Trainer.
对于武器，你需要在弹药商店购买，不能通过训练师生成（或者我不知道如何生成）。
Which bugs can do my life harder?
哪些虫子会让我的生活更艰难？

Carcols.meta/Carvariations.meta ID's: Try changing ID's in both files (If ID is 900, try 953 and other ID's) to see if this helps Tuning Parts working again. Since the DOOMSDAY game update, the limit of IDs is 32767.
Carcols.meta/Carvariations.meta ID：尝试更改两个文件中的 ID（如果 ID 为 900，请尝试 953 和其他 ID），看看这是否有助于调整部件再次工作。自《DOOMSDAY》游戏更新以来，ID限制为32767。
Bad edited files/Incorrect name's: Be sure you edited all files correctly, without mistakes, sometimes that's the problem (Using XML Tools with Notepad++ you can find if you did any mistake opening/closing tags (Example of a tag: <Item>).
编辑的文件错误/名称不正确：确保您正确编辑了所有文件，没有错误，有时这就是问题所在（将 XML 工具与 Notepad++ 一起使用，您可以发现您是否在打开/关闭标签时犯了任何错误（标签示例： <Item> ）。
Why my car has no sound?
为什么我的车没有声音？

In "vehicles.meta" file: Check if "AudioNameHash" tag is like "<AudioNameHash />". If yes, then change it to "<AudioNameHash>VEHICLENAME</AudioNameHash>", where "VEHICLENAME" is the name of the vehicle you like the sound of and you want to use it for your Add-On vehicle.
在“vehicles.meta”文件中：检查“AudioNameHash”标签是否类似于“”。如果是，则将其更改为“VEHICLENAME”，其中“VEHICLENAME”是您喜欢声音的车辆的名称，并且您希望将其用于附加车辆。
Why my game starts crashing when I try to add a new Add-On Folder to DLCPACKS?
为什么当我尝试向 DLCPACKS 添加新的附加文件夹时，我的游戏开始崩溃？

No worries about that: Probably you reached the limit of vehicles added to the game files. You can easily fix that using the gameconfig mentioned below ("What I need before start using this method" section).
不用担心：您可能已达到添加到游戏文件中的车辆限制。您可以使用下面提到的游戏配置轻松解决此问题（“开始使用此方法之前我需要什么”部分）。
Why my game crashes when I try to go into an Add-On vehicle?
为什么当我尝试进入附加载具时，我的游戏会崩溃？

Vehicle Layouts: The game tries to find the correct layouts for the car you spawned but it doesn't find them, so the game crashes because there's no important information.
车辆布局：游戏试图为您生成的汽车找到正确的布局，但没有找到它们，因此游戏崩溃，因为没有重要信息。

How to fix that? You just need to see in which original game car is based the Add-On vehicle you made, look at the "vehiclelayouts.meta" file located to the path where's the original game vehicle, take the info related to it and add it to respective TAGS into the "vehiclelayouts.meta" file located in your Add-On files.
如何解决这个问题？你只需要看看你制作的附加车辆是哪辆原始游戏车，查看位于原始游戏车辆路径的“vehiclelayouts.meta”文件，获取与之相关的信息，并将其添加到相应的 TAGS 中，进入位于附加组件文件中的“vehiclelayouts.meta”文件。

That should fix the problem if you did all correctly.
如果您做对了，这应该可以解决问题。

Where I can find the DATA for each car I want to put as Add-On?
在哪里可以找到我想作为附加组件放置的每辆车的数据？

handling.meta and vehicles.meta: The main ones are located on "/update/update.rpf/common/data/handling.meta" and "/update/update.rpf/common/data/levels/gta5/vehicles.meta", but in case that data is not located in any of both files, you'll have to check the content of every one of that files into each folder inside /update/x64/dlcpacks.
handling.meta 和 vehicles.meta：主要文件位于 "/update/update.rpf/common/data/handling.meta" 和 "/update/update.rpf/common/data/levels/gta5/vehicles.meta" 上，但如果数据不在这两个文件中的任何一个文件中，则必须将每个文件的内容签入其中 /update/x64/dlcpacks 的每个文件夹中。
carcols.meta: You'll have to check every one until you find the correct/needed data for your car. Be sure to check first carcols.ymt too, which is located in /update/update.rpf/x64/data.
carcols.meta：您必须检查每一个，直到找到适合您汽车的正确/所需数据。请务必首先 /update/update.rpf/x64/data 检查位于 .
carvariations.meta: You can take any of the available ones and change just the lines needed (Always change the line that contains the car name with the new one, and if car does not have tuning parts in <kits> section, change the line inside it to <Item>0_default_modkit</Item>.)
carvariations.meta：您可以采用任何可用的行并仅更改所需的行（始终将包含汽车名称的行更改为新行，如果汽车在部分中没有 <kits> 调整部件，请将其内部的行更改为 <Item>0_default_modkit</Item> .）
My vehicle have some strange/missplaced corona's on headlights and taillights, how I fix that?
我的车辆在大灯和尾灯上有一些奇怪/错位的电晕，我该如何解决？

That's pretty easy, just open your carvariations.meta file with Notepad++ or any other text editor and replace the line similar to <lightSettings value="918" /> ("918" value can be another value in your case) with <lightSettings value="0" />. This will remove that shit tailights and will align headlights.
这很简单，只需使用 Notepad++ 或任何其他文本编辑器打开您的 carvariations.meta 文件，然后将类似于 <lightSettings value="918" /> （“918”值在您的情况下可以是另一个值）的行替换为 <lightSettings value="0" /> .这将消除那些狗屎灯，并将对齐大灯。
Knowledge: What I need before start using this method?
Knowledge ： 在开始使用此方法之前，我需要什么？
[OpenIV](http://openiv.com/) (Mandatory) OpenIV（必填）
[NVE's Gameconfig](https://www.razedmods.com/gta-v) (MUST-HAVE to avoid game crashes). You will download the full mod but you only need to get the gameconfig from the OPTIONALS folder that's inside the package. Has been hard tested and works perfectly fine in every case.
NVE 的 Gameconfig（必须避免游戏崩溃）。您将下载完整的模组，但您只需要从包内的 OPTIONALS 文件夹中获取游戏配置。经过严格测试，在每种情况下都能正常工作。
[Notepad++](https://notepad-plus-plus.org/download/v6.9.2.html) or any other text editor (Mandatory)
Notepad++ 或任何其他文本编辑器（必填）
Keep calm during the process (Mandatory)
在此过程中保持冷静（必填）
Knowledge: What contains Add-On/Replace Base Folder?
Knowledge ：什么包含附加/替换基本文件夹？
File Name 文件名	Description 描述	Knowledge 知识
VEHICLES 车辆	
Vehicles DLC Folder Vehicles DLC 文件夹	You'll need to edit normal META files and add vehicles files as always, but also edit "content.xml" file each time you add Tuning Parts for any car.
您需要像往常一样编辑普通的 META 文件并添加车辆文件，但每次为任何汽车添加改装零件时，还需要编辑“content.xml”文件。
Basic 基本
Vehicles DLC Folder #:two: Vehicles DLC 文件夹#	You won't need to edit "content.xml" file. That's because with this method you only need to put tuning part files (NO entire vehiclename_mods.rpf files, YES .ytd/.ytf one's) on tuning_mods.rpf file.
您无需编辑“content.xml”文件。这是因为使用这种方法，您只需要将调整部分文件（没有整个 vehiclename_mods.rpf 文件，是的 .ytd/.ytf ）放在 tuning_mods.rpf 文件中。
Medium 中等
Vehicles DLC Folder #:four: Vehicles DLC 文件夹#	Is almost the same as the first one, BUT, with this, you'll be able to use MPLUXE vehicles as Add-On's, like Pagani Huayra by Vans123. Also, now you can add vehicles from MPHEIST, like M1116 Humvee by SkylineGTRFreak without crashes and totally functional. That's something that with the first one you can't do, otherwise your game will crash.
与第一个几乎相同，但是，有了这个，您将能够将 MPLUXE 车辆用作附加组件，例如 Vans123 的 Pagani Huayra。此外，现在您可以从 MPHEIST 添加车辆，例如 SkylineGTRFreak 的 M1116 悍马，而不会发生碰撞且功能齐全。这是第一个你不能做的事情，否则你的游戏就会崩溃。
Advanced 高深
WEAPONS 武器	
Weapons DLC Folder 武器DLC文件夹	Here you can put melee weapons. Don't try with gunfire weapons, won't work.
在这里你可以放置近战武器。不要尝试使用枪击武器，这是行不通的。
Basic 基本
Melee Weapons DLC Folder 近战武器DLC文件夹	Same as before, but this one is provided by @yeahhmonkey and should work better.
和以前一样，但这个是由@yeahhmonkey提供的，应该可以更好地工作。
Basic 基本
Assault Weapons DLC Folder
突击武器DLC文件夹
Here you can put only Assault (gunfire) weapons. Again provided by @yeahhmonkey.
在这里，您只能放置突击（枪击）武器。再次由@yeahhmonkey提供。
Basic 基本
Before you use the tutorial below, remember that if you want to convert a "mpluxe" Replacer car mod like Pagani Huayra by Vans123 to an Add-On, you should use "Vehicles DLC Folder #:four:" from my [Add-On / Replace Base Folder](https://es.gta5-mods.com/tools/add-on-replace-base-folder) mod. (MOST RECOMMENDED OPTION)
在使用下面的教程之前，请记住，如果您想将 Vans123 的 Pagani Huayra 等“mpluxe”Replacer 汽车模组转换为附加组件，您应该使用我的附加组件/替换基础文件夹模组中的“车辆 DLC 文件夹 #”。（最推荐的选项）

___________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________

Tutorial: CREATE YOUR OWN ADD-ON PACK
Tutorial ：创建自己的附加包
BEFORE YOU START: If is the first time you will do an Add-On Pack, follow all the steps below. When you complete that, verify that your Add-On is working fine before you add more vehicles into it.
BEFORE YOU START: 如果这是您第一次制作附加包，请按照以下所有步骤操作。完成此操作后，请先验证您的附加组件是否正常工作，然后再向其添加更多车辆。

IF YOU ALREADY HAVE AN ADD-ON WHERE YOU WOULD LIKE TO ADD MORE CARS: In that case, just start directly from the Step :six: (Don't forget to read the WARNING that's just above this Step).
IF YOU ALREADY HAVE AN ADD-ON WHERE YOU WOULD LIKE TO ADD MORE CARS: 在这种情况下，只需直接从步骤 （ Don't forget to read the WARNING that's just above this Step ） 开始。

Step :one:: [Download this file as a base for your Add-On's](https://es.gta5-mods.com/tools/add-on-replace-base-folder).
步骤：下载此文件作为附加组件的基础。

Step :two:: Once downloaded, unzip to anywhere you want.
步骤：下载后，解压缩到您想要的任何位置。

Step :three:: Now, open OpenIV, go to "/mods/update/x64/dlcpacks/", create a new folder called as you want (I usually call my packs as "A2NS", "A2NS2", "A2NS3", etc) and put inside the "dlc.rpf" file.
步骤：现在，打开OpenIV，转到“ ”，根据需要创建一个新文件夹（我通常将我的包称为“A2NS”、“A2NS2”、“A2NS3”等）并放入“ /mods/update/x64/dlcpacks/ dlc.rpf”文件中。

Step :four:: Go back to "/mods/update/". Now, go to "/update.rpf/common/data/" and export "dlclist.xml" to anywhere you want on your system.
步骤：返回“ /mods/update/ ”。现在，转到“ ”并将“ /update.rpf/common/data/ dlclist.xml”导出到系统上所需的任何位置。

Step :five:: Use a text editor as [Notepad++](https://notepad-plus-plus.org/download/v6.9.2.html) and edit the file with the next line (Change FOLDERNAME to the name you put to your DLC BASE Folder):
步骤：使用文本编辑器作为Notepad ++，并使用下一行编辑文件（将FOLDERNAME更改为您添加到DLC BASE文件夹的名称）：

For "dlclist.xml": 对于“dlclist.xml”：

	<Item>dlcpacks:\FOLDERNAME\</Item>        
And now, save changes and put it back to directory mentioned in Step :four:.
现在，保存更改并将其放回步骤中提到的目录。

IMPORTANT: Edit "content.xml", and "setup2.xml", changing each "FOLDERNAME" word that you find in each file with the word you use as name for your Add-On's folder. Else, your game will crash.
重要说明：编辑“content.xml”和“setup2.xml”，将每个文件中找到的每个“FOLDERNAME”单词更改为用作附加组件文件夹名称的单词。否则，您的游戏将崩溃。

Now you have a BASE folder to put replace cars files and data inside as Add-On's.
现在你有一个BASE文件夹，可以把替换汽车的文件和数据作为附加组件放在里面。

WARNING: Before that Step, if your car's already renamed or the name of his files is different to any other car from the game, you don't need to rename them again.
WARNING: 在这一步之前，如果你的汽车已经重命名，或者他的文件名称与游戏中的任何其他汽车不同，你不需要再次重命名它们。

Step :six:: Is the moment to put files into their respective directories. Rename "car.ytf/.ytd" files, for example "chall.ytd/.ytf" (Chall = Challenger), and put them into "/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehicles.rpf". Do the same process with "car_mods.rpf" files, but put them into ""/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehiclemods" (Don't forget to rename files inside "car_mods.rpf", otherwise, they'll conflict with the replacer car tuning parts).
步骤：是将文件放入各自目录的时刻。重命名“car.ytf/.ytd”文件，例如“chall.ytd/.ytf”（Chall = Challenger），并将它们放入“ /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehicles.rpf ”。对“car_mods.rpf”文件执行相同的过程，但将它们放入“” /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehiclemods “中（不要忘记重命名”car_mods.rpf“中的文件，否则它们会与替换汽车改装部件发生冲突）。

Step :seven:: Add DATA from the new car (if the car you want to put as Add-On didn't have data when you downloaded it, take data from the original game car that it replaces) to "vehicles.meta", "carcols.meta", carvariations.meta" and "handling.meta", which located in "/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/data/" editing them with any text editor (This path is supposed to be the place where the DATA files (.meta) of your Add-On should be).
步骤：将新车的 DATA（如果要作为附加组件放置的汽车在下载时没有数据，请从它替换的原始游戏汽车中获取数据）添加到“vehicles.meta”、“carcols.meta”、“carvariations.meta”和“handling.meta”，它们位于“ /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/data/ ”使用任何文本编辑器编辑它们（此路径应该是附加组件的 DATA 文件 （.meta） 应该在的位置）。

Step :eight: (SKIP this if your car doesn't have Tuning Parts): Once you did steps above, if some of the cars you added have Tuning Parts (car_mods.rpf), now go back to "/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/", export "content.xml" file, edit with Notepad++ or any other editor and add these lines to their respective section:
步骤（如果您的汽车没有改装零件，请跳过此步骤）：完成上述步骤后，如果您添加的某些汽车具有改装零件 （car_mods.rpf），现在返回“ ”，导出“ /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/ content.xml”文件，使用 Notepad++ 或任何其他编辑器进行编辑，并将这些行添加到各自的部分：

For "<dataFiles>" section:
对于“”部分：

	<Item> 
          <filename>dlc_FOLDERNAME:/%PLATFORM%/vehiclemods/car_mods.rpf</filename> 
          <fileType>RPF_FILE</fileType> 
          <locked value="true"/>
          <disabled value="true"/>
          <persistent value="true"/>
          <overlay value="true"/>
        </Item>
For "<filesToEnable>" section:
对于“”部分：

	<Item>dlc_FOLDERNAME:/%PLATFORM%/vehiclemods/car_mods.rpf</Item>        
Finally, if you did all correctly, you can try your new Add-On cars
最后，如果你做对了，你可以尝试你的新附加车
;)

Tutorial: REPLACER to ADD-ON Vehicles
Tutorial ： 附加车辆的替代品
Step :one:: [Download this file as a base for your Add-On's](https://es.gta5-mods.com/tools/add-on-replace-base-folder).
步骤：下载此文件作为附加组件的基础。

Step :two:: Once downloaded, unzip to anywhere you want.
步骤：下载后，解压缩到您想要的任何位置。

Step :three:: Now, open OpenIV, go to "/mods/update/x64/dlcpacks/", create a new folder called as you want and put inside the "dlc.rpf" file.
步骤：现在，打开OpenIV，转到“ ”，根据需要创建一个新文件夹，并将其放入“ /mods/update/x64/dlcpacks/ dlc.rpf”文件中。

Step :four:: Go back to "/mods/update/". Now, go to "/update.rpf/common/data/" and export "dlclist.xml" to anywhere you want on your system.
步骤：返回“ /mods/update/ ”。现在，转到“ ”并将“ /update.rpf/common/data/ dlclist.xml”导出到系统上所需的任何位置。

Step :five:: Use a text editor as [Notepad++](https://notepad-plus-plus.org/download/v6.9.2.html) and edit the file with the next line (Change FOLDERNAME to the name you put to your DLC BASE Folder):
步骤：使用文本编辑器作为Notepad ++，并使用下一行编辑文件（将FOLDERNAME更改为您添加到DLC BASE文件夹的名称）：

For "dlclist.xml": 对于“dlclist.xml”：

	<Item>dlcpacks:\FOLDERNAME\</Item>        
And now, save changes and put it back to directory mentioned in Step :four:.
现在，保存更改并将其放回步骤中提到的目录。

IMPORTANT: Edit "content.xml", and "setup2.xml", changing each "FOLDERNAME" word that you find in each file with the word you use as name for your Add-On's folder. Otherwise, your game will crash.
重要说明：编辑“content.xml”和“setup2.xml”，将每个文件中找到的每个“FOLDERNAME”单词更改为用作附加组件文件夹名称的单词。否则，您的游戏将崩溃。

Now you have a BASE folder to put replace cars files and data inside as Add-On's.
现在你有一个BASE文件夹，可以把替换汽车的文件和数据作为附加组件放在里面。

Step :six:: Is the moment to put files into their respective directories. Rename "car.ytf/.ytd" files, for example "chall.ytd/.ytf" (Chall = Challenger), and put them into "/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehicles.rpf". Do the same process with "car_mods.rpf" files, but put them into ""/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehiclemods" (Don't forget to rename files inside "car_mods.rpf", otherwise, they'll conflict with the replacer car tuning parts).
步骤：是将文件放入各自目录的时刻。重命名“car.ytf/.ytd”文件，例如“chall.ytd/.ytf”（Chall = Challenger），并将它们放入“ /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehicles.rpf ”。对“car_mods.rpf”文件执行相同的过程，但将它们放入“” /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehiclemods “中（不要忘记重命名”car_mods.rpf“中的文件，否则它们会与替换汽车改装部件发生冲突）。

Step :seven:: Add DATA from replacer cars (if the car you want to put as Add-On didn't have data when you downloaded it, take data from the original game car that it replaces) to "vehicles.meta", "carcols.meta", carvariations.meta" and "handling.meta", which located in "/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/data/" editing them with any text editor.
步骤：将替换汽车的数据（如果要作为附加组件放置的汽车在下载时没有数据，请从它替换的原始游戏汽车中获取数据）添加到“vehicles.meta”，“carcols.meta”，carvariations.meta“和”handling.meta“，它们位于” /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/data/ “使用任何文本编辑器编辑它们。

Step :eight: (SKIP this if your car doesn't have Tuning Parts): Once you did steps above, if some of the cars you added have Tuning Parts (car_mods.rpf), now go back to "/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/", export "content.xml" file, edit with Notepad++ or any other editor and add these lines to their respective section:
步骤（如果您的汽车没有改装零件，请跳过此步骤）：完成上述步骤后，如果您添加的某些汽车具有改装零件 （car_mods.rpf），现在返回“ ”，导出“ /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/ content.xml”文件，使用 Notepad++ 或任何其他编辑器进行编辑，并将这些行添加到各自的部分：

For "<dataFiles>" section:
对于“”部分：

	<Item> 
          <filename>dlc_FOLDERNAME:/%PLATFORM%/vehiclemods/car_mods.rpf</filename> 
          <fileType>RPF_FILE</fileType> 
          <locked value="true"/>
          <disabled value="true"/>
          <persistent value="true"/>
          <overlay value="true"/>
        </Item>
For "<filesToEnable>" section:
对于“”部分：

	<Item>dlc_FOLDERNAME:/%PLATFORM%/vehiclemods/car_mods.rpf</Item>        
Finally, if you did all correctly, you can try your new Add-On cars
最后，如果你做对了，你可以尝试你的新附加车
;)

Tutorial: ADD-ON to REPLACER Vehicles
Tutorial ： REPLACER Vehicles 的附加组件
BEFORE YOU START: If it's the first time you will do a replace vehicles folder, follow all the steps below. When you complete that, verify that your replace vehicle is working fine before you add more vehicles into it.
BEFORE YOU START: 如果这是您第一次执行替换车辆文件夹，请按照以下所有步骤操作。完成此操作后，请先验证更换的车辆是否工作正常，然后再添加更多车辆。

There will be an already made replace folder in the final of this section, in case that you want to compare your results with my own folder.
在本节的最后将有一个已经制作的替换文件夹，以防您想将结果与我自己的文件夹进行比较。

Step :one:: First, you need to download your desired file, for example, let's take the [Ford GT 2005 by Aige](https://es.gta5-mods.com/vehicles/2005-ford-gt-aige).
步骤：首先，您需要下载所需的文件，例如，让我们以 Aige 的福特 GT 2005 为例。

Step :two:: Once you have the mod downloaded, unzip and open "dlc.rpf" file with OpenIV.
步骤：下载mod后，使用OpenIV解压缩并打开“dlc.rpf”文件。

Step :three:: Find the "fgt.ytd", "fgt.ytf" and "fgt_hi.ytf" files using Ctrl + F3 and export these files anywhere you want. Do the same but with "fgt_mods.rpf" file. (Don't close "dlc.rpf" file opened with OpenIV yet, because we'll take the metadata information for Tuning Parts later on).
步骤：使用 Ctrl + F3 找到“fgt.ytd”、“fgt.ytf”和“fgt_hi.ytf”文件，并将这些文件导出到您想要的任何位置。执行相同的操作，但使用“fgt_mods.rpf”文件。（不要关闭使用 OpenIV 打开的“dlc.rpf”文件，因为我们稍后将获取 Tuning Parts 的元数据信息）。

Step :four:: Rename the exported "fgt.ytd", "fgt.ytf", "fgt_hi.ytf" and "fgt_mods.rpf" files to "bullet.ytd", "bullet.ytf", "bullet_hi.ytf" and "bullet_mods.rpf" respectively. These are the files that will replace the BULLET game vehicle and its tuning with the Ford GT 2005 models that you've downloaded previously.
步骤：将导出的“fgt.ytd”、“fgt.ytf”、“fgt_hi.ytf”和“fgt_mods.rpf”文件分别重命名为“bullet.ytd”、“bullet.ytf”、“bullet_hi.ytf”和“bullet_mods.rpf”。这些文件将替换 BULLET 游戏车辆及其与您之前下载的福特 GT 2005 模型的调整。

Step :five:: [Download this file as a base for your Add-On's](https://es.gta5-mods.com/tools/add-on-replace-base-folder).
步骤：下载此文件作为附加组件的基础。

Step :six:: Once downloaded, unzip to anywhere you want.
步骤：下载后，解压缩到您想要的任何位置。

Step :seven:: Now, open OpenIV, go to "/mods/update/x64/dlcpacks/", create a new folder called as you want (I usually call my packs as "A2NS", "A2NS2", "A2NS3", etc) and put inside the "dlc.rpf" file of the option #4.
步骤：现在，打开OpenIV，转到“ ”，根据需要创建一个新文件夹（我通常将我的包称为“A2NS”，“A2NS2”，“A2NS3”等）并放入选项#4的“ /mods/update/x64/dlcpacks/ dlc.rpf”文件中。

Step :eight:: Go back to "/mods/update/". Now, go to "/update.rpf/common/data/" and export "dlclist.xml" to anywhere you want on your system.
步骤：返回“ /mods/update/ ”。现在，转到“ ”并将“ /update.rpf/common/data/ dlclist.xml”导出到系统上所需的任何位置。

Step :nine:: Use a text editor as [Notepad++](https://notepad-plus-plus.org/download/v6.9.2.html) and edit the file with the next line (Change FOLDERNAME to the name you put to your new folder):
步骤：使用文本编辑器作为Notepad ++，并使用下一行编辑文件（将FOLDERNAME更改为您放入新文件夹的名称）：

For "dlclist.xml": 对于“dlclist.xml”：

	<Item>dlcpacks:\FOLDERNAME\</Item>        
And now, save changes and put it back to the directory mentioned in Step :seven:.
现在，保存更改并将其放回步骤中提到的目录。

IMPORTANT: Edit "content.xml", and "setup2.xml", changing each "FOLDERNAME" word that you find in each file with the word you use as name for your Add-On's folder. Otherwise your game will crash.
重要说明：编辑“content.xml”和“setup2.xml”，将每个文件中找到的每个“FOLDERNAME”单词更改为用作附加组件文件夹名称的单词。否则，您的游戏将崩溃。

Now you have a BASE folder to put replace cars files and data inside as Add-On's, but they will still replace the game vehicles that's the best part of this process.
现在你有一个 BASE 文件夹，可以将替换汽车文件和数据作为附加组件放入其中，但它们仍然会替换游戏车辆，这是这个过程最好的部分。

Step :keycap_ten:: Is the moment to put the files into their respective directories. Put the exported vehicle files (the "bullet.ytd", "bullet.ytf" and "bullet_hi.ytf" files) into "/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehicles.rpf" (Remember that "FOLDERNAME" is the name of your folder!). Do the same process with the "bullet_mods.rpf" file, but put it into ""/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehiclemods".
步骤：是将文件放入各自目录的时刻。将导出的车辆文件（“bullet.ytd”、“bullet.ytf”和“bullet_hi.ytf”文件）放入“ /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehicles.rpf ”（请记住，“FOLDERNAME”是您的文件夹名称！对“bullet_mods.rpf”文件执行相同的过程，但将其放入“” /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/x64/vehiclemods 中。

Step :one::one:: Add the metadata information from the new car to the "carcols.meta" and "carvariations.meta" files respectively, which are located in "/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/data/" editing them with any text editor (This path is supposed to be the place where the metadata files (.meta) of your replace folder should be).
步骤：将新车的元数据信息分别添加到“carcols.meta”和“carvariations.meta”文件中，这些文件位于“ /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/data/ ”使用任何文本编辑器编辑它们（此路径应该是替换文件夹的元数据文件（.meta）的位置）。

WARNING: The "vehicles.meta" and "handling.meta" files won't work there. These files should be edited on the following path:
WARNING: “vehicles.meta”和“handling.meta”文件在那里不起作用。应在以下路径上编辑这些文件：

Path for "handling.meta" file: "mods/update/update.rpf/common/data/"
“handling.meta”文件的路径：” mods/update/update.rpf/common/data/
Path for "vehicles.meta" file: "mods/update/update.rpf/common/data/levels/gta5/"
“vehicles.meta”文件的路径：” mods/update/update.rpf/common/data/levels/gta5/
Step :one::two:: Now it's the time to edit the previous metadata information files. Do this process for all of them (except "handling.meta" and "vehicles.meta" files, which should be edited in a different way):
步骤：现在是编辑以前的元数据信息文件的时候了。对所有这些文件（“handling.meta”和“vehicles.meta”文件除外，应以不同的方式进行编辑）执行此过程：

Open the file and search for the word "fgt". You should find, at least, one result or more depending on which file you're editing.
打开文件并搜索单词“fgt”。您应该至少找到一个或多个结果，具体取决于您正在编辑的文件。
Replace the found word/s with "bullet" until there's not any "fgt" word left.
将找到的单词替换为“bullet”，直到没有任何“fgt”单词。
Save the changes and do the same process for every metadata file.
保存更改，并对每个元数据文件执行相同的过程。
For the handling.meta and vehicles.meta files, instead of renaming we will do the following:
对于 handling.meta 和 vehicles.meta 文件，我们将执行以下操作，而不是重命名：

Export both files anywhere you want. Open them and find the "bullet" lines.
将这两个文件导出到您想要的任何位置。打开它们并找到“项目符号”行。
From the first "<item>" to the first "</item>" open/close tags of the "bullet" find, replace the content with the same lines provided by the Add-On file that you've downloaded, but remember to keep the name "bullet".
从“bullet”查找的第一个“”到第一个“”打开/关闭标记，将内容替换为已下载的附加组件文件提供的相同行，但请记住保留名称“bullet”。
Once it's done, import them again to the respective paths.
完成后，再次将它们导入到相应的路径中。

Step :one::three:: Once you did steps above, now go back to "/FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/", export "content.xml" file, edit with Notepad++ or any other editor and add these lines to their respective section:
步骤：完成上述步骤后，现在返回“ ”，导出“ /FOLDERNAME/dlc.rpf/ content.xml”文件，使用Notepad ++或任何其他编辑器进行编辑，并将这些行添加到各自的部分：

For "<dataFiles>" section:
对于“”部分：

	<Item> 
          <filename>dlc_FOLDERNAME:/%PLATFORM%/vehiclemods/bullet_mods.rpf</filename> 
          <fileType>RPF_FILE</fileType> 
          <locked value="true"/>
          <disabled value="true"/>
          <persistent value="true"/>
          <overlay value="true"/>
        </Item>
For "<filesToEnable>" section:
对于“”部分：

	<Item>dlc_FOLDERNAME:/%PLATFORM%/vehiclemods/bullet_mods.rpf</Item>        
Finally, if you did all correctly, you can try your new Add-On cars working as replacers without having to mess with most of the original game files
最后，如果你做对了一切，你可以尝试你的新附加汽车作为替代品，而不必弄乱大多数原始游戏文件
;)

在这里下载我制作的例子

Tutorial: REPLACER to ADD-ON MELEE Weapons
Tutorial ：ADD-ON MELEE Weapons 的替代品
:anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger: WARNING  警告:anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger:
Never tried to put weapons as Add-On's, so if something does not work correctly with yours, remember that these steps are only for MELEE weapons, and maybe won't work for other weapons type.
从来没有尝试过将武器作为附加组件，所以如果某些东西不能正常工作，请记住这些步骤仅适用于近战武器，可能不适用于其他武器类型。

If you have any doubt about this method, please ask to @yeahhmonkey, he was who got it working, I only helped a bit in the process.
如果您对这种方法有任何疑问，请询问@yeahhmonkey，他是让它工作的人，我只是在这个过程中帮了一点忙。

:anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger::anger:
Before you start with steps, I recommend use [this method to follow the process](https://es.gta5-mods.com/weapons/add-on-melee-weapon-base), otherwise this method could not work for you.
在开始步骤之前，我建议使用此方法遵循该过程，否则此方法将不适合您。

STEPS: 步骤：

Step :one:: First, you need to download your desired MELEE weapon file.
步骤：首先，您需要下载所需的近战武器文件。

Step :two:: Once you have the mod downloaded, unzip and take "weapon.ytd/.ytf" files. Open OpenIV and go to "/dlc.rpf/x64/models/cdimages/weapons.rpf" and put these files there.
步骤： 下载模组后，解压缩并获取“weapon.ytd/.ytf”文件。打开 OpenIV 并转到“ /dlc.rpf/x64/models/cdimages/weapons.rpf ”并将这些文件放在那里。

Step :three:: Go to "/dlc.rpf/common/data" and add DATA from the Replacer weapon (take it from original Rockstar Game files or if weapon comes with his own, use it) to each file of this location, and don't forget to do the same if needed with "/ai" and "anim" folders inside the previous one, but mainly they shouldn't be edited.
步骤：转到“ ”并将替换武器中的DATA（从原始Rockstar Game文件中获取，或者如果武器自带，请使用它）添加到此位置的每个文件中，如果需要，请不要忘记对前一个文件夹中的“/ai”和“ /dlc.rpf/common/data anim”文件夹执行相同的操作，但主要是它们不应该被编辑。

(Don't forget to replace "FOLDER" word in all the files that have it with the name of your DLC folder.) (Be sure you're doing all correctly, please, be careful with this step).
（不要忘记将包含它的所有文件中的“FOLDER”单词替换为您的 DLC 文件夹的名称。（请确保你做对了，请小心这一步）。

Step :four:: Now go to "/dlc.rpf/", edit "content.xml" and "setup2.xml" files and change each "FOLDER" word with the name of your new DLC folder (if you changed it, obviously, otherwise don't do that).
步骤：现在转到“/dlc.rpf/”，编辑“content.xml”和“setup2.xml”文件，并使用新DLC文件夹的名称更改每个“FOLDER”单词（如果您更改了它，显然，否则不要这样做）。

Step :five:: Use a text editor as [Notepad++](https://notepad-plus-plus.org/download), edit "dlclist.xml" file in "/mods/update/update.rpf/common/data" with this line (Change FOLDER to name you put to your DLC BASE Folder):
步骤：使用文本编辑器作为记事本++，编辑“ ” /mods/update/update.rpf/common/data 中的“dlclist.xml”文件，并使用此行（将FOLDER更改为您放入DLC BASE文件夹的名称）：

For "dlclist.xml": 对于“dlclist.xml”：

	<Item>dlcpacks:\FOLDER\</Item>

Tutorial: ADD-ON to REPLACE - MELEE Weapons
Tutorial ： REPLACE - 近战武器
This method is very simple and you have 2 ways to do it, just use ONE of the below (I really recommend the FIRST WAY, is the easiest and fastest one):
这种方法非常简单，您有 2 种方法可以做到这一点，只需使用以下方法之一（我真的推荐第一种方法，这是最简单和最快的一种）：
FIRST WAY (Highly Recommended):
第一种方式（强烈推荐）：

Step :one:: Change all "weapon.ytd/.ytf" name files to an existing one. For example, if you have an knife called "knifeADD" and you want it as replacer for the original "Knife" of the game, just change his ".ytd/.ytf" names to "Knife.ytd/.ytf", and it will appear as replacer.
步骤：将所有“weapon.ytd/.ytf”名称文件更改为现有文件。例如，如果你有一把名为“knifeADD”的刀，并且希望它作为游戏原始“刀”的替代品，只需将他的“.ytd/.ytf”名称更改为“Knife.ytd/.ytf”，它就会显示为替代品。

Step :two:: Taking the example above, open every DATA file of the Add-On, and change any "knifeADD" name found into them with the "knife" word. This will make that "knifeADD" data now will work for "knife" weapon.
步骤：以上面的示例为例，打开附加组件的每个 DATA 文件，并使用“knife”一词更改其中找到的任何“knifeADD”名称。这将使“knifeADD”数据现在适用于“刀”武器。

SECOND WAY (Much more stressfull. Only for people with a lot of free time and patience):
第二种方式（压力更大。仅适用于有很多空闲时间和耐心的人）：

Step :one:: Rename "knifeADD" (taking the First Way EXAMPLE) weapon files located in "/dlc.rpf/x64/models/cdimages/weapons.rpf" to "knife" and place them to the "knife" original game location files (Use Ctrl + F3 with OpenIV to find them).
步骤：将位于“ ”中的“knifeADD”（以第一种方式为例）武器文件重命名为“knife”，并将它们放置到“ /dlc.rpf/x64/models/cdimages/weapons.rpf knife”原始游戏位置文件中（使用OpenIV的Ctrl + F3来查找它们）。

Step :two: (Stressfull): Change all "knifeADD" words inside each DATA file to "knife". Then copy/paste every DATA lines from every DATA file to his respective file located in any of the "patchdayXng", replacing old lines.
步骤（Stressfull）：将每个 DATA 文件中的所有“knifeADD”单词更改为“knife”。然后将每个 DATA 文件中的每个 DATA 行复制/粘贴到位于任何“patchdayXng”中的相应文件中，替换旧行。

You finished!! 你完成了！！ :grinning:

POLL: ¿How can I improve this tutorial?
POLL ： ¿如何改进本教程？
You're free to help me improve this tutorial or help others, as @yeahhmonkey and more awesome people did already ;).
您可以自由地帮助我改进本教程或帮助其他人，就像@yeahhmonkey和更多很棒的人所做的那样。

I want to convert this tutorial as a base/resource for GTA V modding, so, if you have more information about other GTA V errors, please provide it to me or add a comment here, so I can read and add it to this Tutorial.
我想将本教程转换为 GTA V 改装的基础/资源，因此，如果您有关于其他 GTA V 错误的更多信息，请将其提供给我或在此处添加评论，以便我可以阅读并将其添加到本教程中。

To make it easier, just copy/paste and replace the following lines of code with the specific information on each part:
为了方便起见，只需复制/粘贴以下代码行，并将其替换为每个部分的特定信息：

- **`ERROR NAME HERE`:** Definition about why it happens here (If you have no idea, write VOID). 
***How to fix that?*** Here your explanation about how to fix it (If you have no idea, write VOID).
___________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________________

If I missed something or you're having problems using this method, please leave a comment.

[Reyser](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/user/reyser) [ MODERATOR](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/groups/global-moderators) [7 years ago](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/post/1296)  
@LeeC2202 extratitleupdatedata is a file used by Rockstar to patch files for their DLCs, it's a better way than downloading entire DLC/'s again each time they update or add something. If you'll add more cars in the future, don't use it, is not needed for us, just for Rockstar.
@LeeC2202 extratitleupdatedata 是 Rockstar 用来修补其 DLC 文件的文件，但这比每次更新或添加内容时再次下载整个 DLC 更好。如果将来要添加更多汽车，请不要使用它，我们不需要它，只是为了 Rockstar。

[Reyser](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/user/reyser) [ MODERATOR](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/groups/global-moderators) [7 years ago](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/post/1342) 
@yeahhmonkey There are a lot of files for weapons Data, so, you can use "Ctrl + F3" and check which of them have Knife DATA, then, take this data and put it on your DLC folder file respectivelly, an example:

If there are 8 "shop_weapon.meta" using Ctrl + F3, check each one until you find the weapon data you're searching. If no data, then don't put anything on the respective file of your "/common/data/file.meta". Do the same with all files, except "dlctext.meta", with this one don't do anything.
I don't know if you understand what I'm trying to explain, but is not hard. Also, you can take a look at [this mod](https://es.gta5-mods.com/weapons/mg-42-add-on-replace), is an Add-On weapon (you can see how is structured each file).

[Fearnoid](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/user/fearnoid) [7 years ago](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/post/1580) 
Hello. Very nice tutorial. It's ver helpful.
I just need a little of assistance. It might be a Noob-y question.

First Question. I want to replace my vehicles. I'm using the add-on to replace method. Step 7 is where I usually get confused. So, from my ford GT dlc.rpf I have extracted the nessesary meta files.
I understand that I'm supposed to copy + paste the text from them into the meta files located in the "DLCFolderThatIChose".rpf.
Now what I want to know is, do I copy the text inside <item></item> tags from the fordGT meta files and paste them within the parent tags of the destination meta file?
Or can I simply copy everything inside it the FordGT meta file (including the "vehicleModelInfoVariation" & "?XML version" etc tags) and paste it at the bottom of the destination meta files?
Because the Ford GT has successfully replaced the bullet, and works well, but the tunning & dials don't work.
Second question, inside the meta files for the Ford GT, I've noticed that it has fgt, fgt_modkit & or <modelName>fgt</modelName> keywords. Shouldn't I change them to bullet or something like that?
I know that I'm supposed to to that for the handling meta, but I'm not too sure about the other metas.
Thanks for clearing my doubts. And keep up the great work. :trophy:

 0  
[Reyser](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/user/reyser) [ MODERATOR](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/groups/global-moderators) [7 years ago](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/post/1581)  
[@Fearnoid](https://forums.gta5-mods.com/uid/1650)

Answer to first question: To get dials, lights and tuning working, search for the car name (if is Ford GT to Bullet, in each meta file (if are "fgt.ytd/.ytf" files, then search for "fgt") search it and copy from <Item> to </Item>. Also don't forget that in "carcols.meta" files sometimes there are 2 sections, <Kits></Kits> and <Lights></Lights>. If so, copy both "<Item> to </Item>" lines on their respective section. ALSO, don't forget to replace the "fgt" word with "bullet" of the car you want to replace if you copy the entire <Item> to </Item> lines).

Answer to second question: For "handling.meta" file, first search by car name, and then, search and copy since the first line starting with "<fMass" tag to the "</Item>" tag. For "vehicles.meta", process is the same as for "handling.meta", BUT, searching and copying since the "<expressionDictName>" to the "</Item>" tag, and also don't forget to copy something like the next, but for the car you're replacing (this is in the final of the "vehicles.meta" file and is necessary to get working dials):

 <Item>
    <parent>vehicles_futo_interior</parent>
    <child>bullet</child>
 </Item>
I don't know if I'm explained good (English isn't my native language), but please let me know if you understood what I told you or not.

Join us in the [5Mods Discord](https://discord.gg/hwYVCmw) -> No GTA:Online. Singleplayer ONLY.
